This has three terms:
1. A sin(t) term
2. A sin(v) term
3. A linear v term

I need to find a candidate that can produce `A*sin(t) + B*sin(v) + C*v` for appropriate constants.

Let me check candidates that involve both sin(t) and sin(v) or functions of v that could yield sin(v).

**Candidate 8**: `c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*v + c3*v + c4*v**3 + c5*sin(c6*t + c7*v + c8)`

Setting c0=0 (kills exp term), c4=0 (kills v³), this gives: `(c2+c3)*v + c5*sin(c6*t + c7*v + c8)`. The sin term is `sin(c6*t + c7*v + c8)` which is a single sin of a linear combination — this can't separate into sin(t) + sin(v).

**Candidate 42**: `c0 + c1*cos(c2*v) + c3*v*sin(c4*t + c5)`

This gives cos(v) and v*sin(t) terms, not sin(v) and sin(t).

**Candidate 1**: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*v²*exp(c4*t) + c5*sin(c6*t + c7*v + c8)` — sin of mixed argument, can't separate.

**Candidate 44**: `c0 + c1*v*cos(c2*t) + c3*cos(c4*log(c5*v² + 1)) + c6*v*sin(c7*t + c8)` — has v*cos(t), cos(log(...)), v*sin(t). None produce sin(v).

**Candidate 14**: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*sin(c3*t + c4)) + c5*sin(c6*t + c7)*cos(c8*v)` — has exp(sin(t)) and sin(t)*cos(v). Using product-to-sum: sin(t)*cos(v) = [sin(t+v) + sin(t-v)]/2. Not helpful.

**Candidate 21**: `c0*t + c1 + c2*t + c3*v^c4*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*cos(c8*v + c9*t)`
Setting c0+c2=0 (no linear t), c1=0, c4=0 gives c3*sin(c5*t+c6) which handles sin(t). Then c7*cos(c8*v + c9*t): setting c9=0 gives c7*cos(c8*v). With c8=1: c7*cos(v). But we need sin(v) + linear v, not cos(v). cos(v) can't give sin(v) + linear v.

**Candidate 33**: `c0*t + c1 + c2*t + c3*v^c4*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*sin(c8*t + c9)`
Setting c0+c2=0, c1=0, c4=0: `c3*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*sin(c8*t + c9)`. Setting c5=1,c6=0: c3*sin(t). Setting c8=0: c7*v*sin(c9). This gives c3*sin(t) + c7*sin(c9)*v. That's sin(t) + const*v. Missing sin(v).

But wait — what if c4=1? Then c3*v*sin(c5*t+c6). Setting c5=0: c3*v*sin(c6). Plus c7*v*sin(c8*t+c9). Setting c8=1, c9=0: c7*v*sin(t). So we get linear_v + v*sin(t), no standalone sin(t) or sin(v).

- No candidate has separate sin(v) and sin(t) terms
- Mixed arguments sin(at + bv) can't decompose into sin(t) + sin(v)
- Terms like cos(v), log(v²+1), exp(v²), v*sin(t) etc. cannot replicate sin(v)
